## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |

| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

## Grafana Database Migration Framework

All relevant Go source files are located in `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/` within `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`:

### Core Files

| File | Role |
|------|------|
| `migrator.go` | **Migration runner** — `Migrator` struct, `RunMigrations`, `run`, `doMigration`, `InTransaction` (rollback), `AddCreateMigration`, `GetMigrationLog`, `MigrationLog` struct |
| `dialect.go` | **SQL dialect abstraction** — `Dialect` interface, `BaseDialect` with default implementations, `NewDialect` factory |
| `mysql_dialect.go` | **MySQL dialect** — `MySQLDialect`, GET_LOCK advisory locking, ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE upsert |
| `postgres_dialect.go` | **PostgreSQL dialect** — `PostgresDialect`, pg_try_advisory_lock, ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert |
| `sqlite_dialect.go` | **SQLite dialect** — `SQLite3`, sqlite_master index checks, ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert |
| `types.go` | `Migration`/`CodeMigration` interfaces, `Table`, `Index`, `DB_*` type constants |
| `column.go` | `Column` struct |
| `conditions.go` | `MigrationCondition` interface and implementations for conditional migrations |
| `migrations.go` | Concrete migration types: `RawSQLMigration`, `AddColumnMigration`, `AddTableMigration`, etc. |
| `dialect_test.go` | Tests for dialect InsertQuery/UpdateQuery |
| `upsert_test.go` | Tests for UpsertMultipleSQL across all dialects |

### Key Design Points
- **Version tracking**: The `migration_log` table (created by `AddCreateMigration`) records each migration's ID, SQL, success status, and timestamp
- **Rollback**: `InTransaction` wraps each migration in a DB transaction with `sess.Rollback()` on error
- **Distributed locking**: MySQL uses `GET_LOCK`/`RELEASE_LOCK`; Po

282026-03-08T22:01:03.462509agentmessage-
The task is complete. I have created `/workspace/answer.json` with a comprehensive mapping of all Go source files that implement the Grafana database migration framework in `sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec`.

The answer covers all four requested components:

1. **Migration runner** → `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go` — contains the `Migrator` struct with `RunMigrations`, `run`, `doMigration`, `exec`, and `InTransaction` methods.

2. **Migration version tracking table** → `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go` — the `MigrationLog` struct maps to the `migration_log` DB table; `AddCreateMigration` creates it; `GetMigrationLog` reads it to skip already-applied migrations.

3. **SQL dialect abstraction** → four files:
   - `dialect.go` — `Dialect` interface + `BaseDialect` base implementation
   - `mysql_dialect.go` — `MySQLDialect`
   - `postgres_dialect.go` — `PostgresDialect`
   - `sqlite_dialect.go` — `SQLite3`

4. **Migration rollback handling** → `pkg/services/sqlstore/migrator/migrator.go` — `InTransaction` wraps each migration in a DB transaction and calls `sess.Rollback()` on error.

Supporting files (`types.go`, `column.go`, `conditions.go`, `migrations.go`, `dialect_test.go`, `upsert_test.go`) are also included for completeness.

the specific name\\\\n278: \\\\t// the lock is exclusive per session and is released explicitly by executing RELEASE_LOCK() or implicitly when the session terminates\\\\n279: \\\\t// it returns 1 if Here is a breakdown of each component:\\n\\n**Migration Runner** (`migrator.go`):\\nThe `Migrator` struct is the central runner. It holds the DB engine, dialect, list of migrations, and the migration log map. Key methods:\\n- `NewMigrator` / `NewScopedMigrator`: constructors that set up the migrator with a dialect chosen by driver name.\\n- `RunMigrations` (and the soft-deprecated `Start`): entry point that optionally acquires a distributed advisory lock (MySQL GET_LOCK / Postgres pg_try_advisory_lock) before calling `run`.\\n- `run`: iterates all registered migrations, skips already-logged ones, and calls `doMigration` for each pending one.\\n- `doMigration` / `exec`: executes a single migration inside a transaction, with retry logic for SQLite busy/locked errors.\\n- `AddMigration`: registers a migration by ID (panics on duplicate IDs).\\n\\n**Migration Version Tracking Table** (`migrator.go`):\\nThe `MigrationLog` struct maps to the `migration_log` database table (or `<scope>_migration_log` for scoped migrators). The table schema is created by `AddCreateMigration`, which adds a `NewAddTableMigration` with columns: `id`, `migration_id`, `sql`, `success`, `error`, `timestamp`. `GetMigrationLog` reads all successful entries from this table into a map keyed by migration ID, which is used to skip already-applied migrations.\\n\\n**SQL Dialect Abstraction** (`dialect.go`, `mysql_dialect.go`, `postgres_dialect.go`, `sqlite_dialect.go`):\\n- `dialect.go`: Defines the `Dialect` interface (with methods for quoting, SQL type mapping, DDL generation, upsert, locking, etc.) and `BaseDialect` which provides default implementations. `NewDialect` is a factory that selects the right dialect by driver name.\\n- `mysql_dialect.go`: `MySQLDialect` implements MySQL-specific SQL (backtick quoting, AUTO_INCREMENT, GET_LOCK/RELEASE_LOCK for advisory locking, ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE upsert).\\n- `postgres_dialect.go`: `PostgresDialect` implements PostgreSQL-specific SQL (double-quote quoting, SERIAL types, pg_try_advisory_lock/pg_advisory_unlock, ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert, ILIKE operator, NULLS FIRST/LAST ordering).\\n- `sqlite_dialect.go`: `SQLite3` implements SQLite-specific SQL (backtick quoting, AUTOINCREMENT, no advisory locking, ON CONFLICT DO UPDATE upsert, sqlite_master index checks).\\n\\n**Migration Rollback Handling** (`migrator.go`):\\nThe `InTransaction` method wraps migration execution in a database transaction. If the migration callback returns an error, `sess.Rollback()` is called to roll back the transaction. This is the primary rollback mechanism. Additionally, the `casRestoreOnErr` helper restores the lock state atomically on error during lock/unlock operations.\\n\\n**Supporting Types**:\\n- `types.go`: Defines the `Migration` and `CodeMigration` interfaces, `Table`, `Index`, and all `DB_*` type constants.\\n- `column.go`: Defines the `Column` struct used in table/migration definitions.\\n- `conditions.go`: Defines `MigrationCondition` interface and implementations (`IfIndexExistsCondition`, `IfIndexNotExistsCondition`, `IfColumnNotExistsCondition`) for conditional migration execution.\\n- `migrations.go`: Concrete migration types: `MigrationBase`, `RawSQLMigration`, `AddColumnMigration`, `RenameColumnMigration`, `AddIndexMigration`, `DropIndexMigration`, `AddTableMigration`, `DropTableMigration`, `RenameTableMigration`, `CopyTableDataMigration`, `TableCharsetMigration`.\\n- `dialect_test.go` and `upsert_test.go`: Test files for the dialect implementations.\"\n}\n",
